+<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8" standalone="yes"?>
+<filters>
+    <filter enabled="true" className="org.omegat.filters2.hhc.HHCFilter2">
+        <files targetFilenamePattern="${filename}" sourceFilenameMask="*.hhc"/>
+        <files targetFilenamePattern="${filename}" sourceFilenameMask="*.hhk"/>
+    </filter>
+    <filter enabled="true" className="org.omegat.filters3.xml.android.AndroidFilter">
+        <files targetFilenamePattern="${filename}" sourceFilenameMask="*.xml"/>
+    </filter>
+    <filter enabled="true" className="org.omegat.filters2.po.PoFilter">
+        <files targetFilenamePattern="${filename}" sourceFilenameMask="*.po"/>
+        <files targetFilenamePattern="${filename}" sourceFilenameMask="*.pot"/>
+    </filter>
+    <filter enabled="true" className="org.omegat.filters2.rc.RcFilter">
+        <files targetEncoding="windows-1251" sourceEncoding="ISO-8859-1" targetFilenamePattern="${filename}" sourceFilenameMask="*.rc"/>
+    </filter>
+    <filter enabled="true" className="org.omegat.filters3.xml.helpandmanual.HelpAndManualFilter">
+        <files targetFilenamePattern="${filename}" sourceFilenameMask="*.xml"/>
+        <files targetFilenamePattern="${filename}" sourceFilenameMask="*.hmxp"/>
+    </filter>
+    <filter enabled="true" className="org.omegat.filters3.xml.resx.ResXFilter">
+        <files targetFilenamePattern="${filename}" sourceFilenameMask="*.resx"/>
+    </filter>
+    <filter enabled="true" className="org.omegat.filters2.xtagqxp.XtagFilter">
+        <files targetEncoding="UTF-16LE" sourceEncoding="UTF-16LE" targetFilenamePattern="${filename}" sourceFilenameMask="*.tag"/>
+        <files targetEncoding="UTF-16LE" sourceEncoding="UTF-16LE" targetFilenamePattern="${filename}" sourceFilenameMask="*.xtg"/>
+    </filter>
+    <filter enabled="true" className="org.omegat.filters3.xml.xliff.XLIFFFilter">
+        <files targetFilenamePattern="${filename}" sourceFilenameMask="*.xlf"/>
+        <files targetFilenamePattern="${filename}" sourceFilenameMask="*.sdlxliff"/>
+    </filter>
